class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">The price of home heating oil and fuel in Northern Ireland is at its lowest level since 2021, and the advice is to buy now – if you are able.</b></p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The average price of 500 litres of home heating oil is £258.78; a litre of petrol costs 128.7p, and diesel is 133.4p per litre, according to <a href="https://www.consumercouncil.org.uk/" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">Consumer Council NI&#x27;s<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> (CCNI) weekly price checker.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In March 2022, 500 litres of home heating oil peaked at £662.86, petrol reached 189.9p per litre in July 2022, and diesel cost an average of 197.5p per litre in June the same year.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Despite the recent warm weather and the incoming summer months, CCNI&#x27;s Head of Energy Raymond Gormley advised &quot;now is a good time&quot; to buy oil in what is a &quot;volatile market&quot;.</p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div the UK nations.</p></div></div><div data-component="subheadline-block" class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0"><h2 id="Fuel-a-good-chunk-of-monthly-wage" I think it&#x27;s the smaller runs. You&#x27;re using a lot more [fuel] because you&#x27;re running back and forth all the time.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;I put about £40 to £50 a week in the car now, as before it was maybe £80 a week.&quot;</p></div></div><div data-component="subheadline-block" class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0"><h2 id="Litre-of-milk-cost-more-concerning" tabindex="-1" class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0"><span role="text">Litre of milk cost &#x27;more concerning&#x27;</span></h2></div><div data-component="image-block" class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-b294mj-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/cpsprodpb/ac90/live/f809d1d0-268e-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/cpsprodpb/ac90/live/f809d1d0-268e-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 320w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/480/cpsprodpb/ac90/live/f809d1d0-268e-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/624/cpsprodpb/ac90/live/f809d1d0-268e-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 624w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/800/cpsprodpb/ac90/live/f809d1d0-268e-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 800w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/976/cpsprodpb/ac90/live/f809d1d0-268e-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 976w" type="image/webp"/><img alt="A man with short brown hair looks into the camera. he said.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;I wouldn&#x27;t be pulling at the pump and looking at the price of a litre of fuel; I&#x27;d be more concerned about the price of a litre of milk.&quot;</p></div></div><div data-component="subheadline-block" class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0"><h2 id="Trump-tariffs-" tabindex="-1" class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0"><span role="text">Trump tariffs </span></h2></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">CCNI&#x27;s Raymond Gormley said the current low prices for fuel and home heating oil were due to several factors, including <a href="/news/articles/c5y66qe404po" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">US President Donald Trump&#x27;s trade tariffs</a> and crude oil producers producing more oil.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The Organisation of the Petroleum Exporting Countries (OPEC), which is an alliance of the top crude oil producers in the world, announced last month they were going to ramp up oil production by 400,000 barrels per day.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;So you take the impact on the world economies that Trump had and that overproduction; it has meant demand is low, supply is high and prices have come down,&quot; said Mr Gormley.</p></div></div><div data-component="image-block" class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-2puule-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/cpsprodpb/d4a2/live/472f1660-269b-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/cpsprodpb/d4a2/live/472f1660-269b-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 320w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/480/cpsprodpb/d4a2/live/472f1660-269b-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/624/cpsprodpb/d4a2/live/472f1660-269b-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 624w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/800/cpsprodpb/d4a2/live/472f1660-269b-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 800w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/976/cpsprodpb/d4a2/live/472f1660-269b-11f0-b26b-ab62c890638b.jpg.webp 976w" type="image/webp"/><img alt="A man with short brown hair smiles and looks into the camera. class="ssrcss-1ml6m0y-Stack e1y4nx260"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">CCNI&#x27;s Raymond Gormley said home heating oil tends to be cheaper in the summer months</p></div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="subheadline-block" class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0"><h2 id="How-much-is-home-heating-oil-and-fuel" tabindex="-1" class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0"><span role="text">How much is home heating oil and fuel?</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-1px28cr-ComponentWrapper-FlourishWrapper eockrme0"><div id="19384787"><div data-component="include-html"><iframe src="https://flo.uri.sh/visualisation/19384787/embed?auto=1" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" height="575" width="700" style="width:100%;" title="Interactive or visual content"></iframe></div></div></div><div class="ssrcss-1px28cr-ComponentWrapper-FlourishWrapper eockrme0"><div id="19384918"><div data-component="include-html"><iframe src="https://flo.uri.sh/visualisation/19384918/embed?auto=1" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" height="575" width="700" style="width:100%;" title="Interactive or visual content"></iframe></div></div></div><div data-component="subheadline-block" class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0"><h2 id="A-really-volatile-market" tabindex="-1" class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0"><span role="text">A really volatile market</span></h2></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Gormley has advised consumers to buy home heating oil if they are able to do so, as it is &quot;good value for money&quot;.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;That&#x27;s not to say it will go down again next week, but equally, it could go up again next week,&quot; he said. &quot;It&#x27;s a really volatile market.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;In the summertime you have 100 different things you want to be spending your money on, and the last thing you want to do is be thinking ahead and going, &#x27;I have a few spare pounds; oil is cheap; I could buy now for the off-season&#x27;.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;It&#x27;s normally cheaper in the summertime than it is in the wintertime because of supply and demand – colder weather, demand is higher and the price goes up.&quot;</p></div></div><div data-component="subheadline-block" class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0"><h2 id="Tips-for-finding-the-cheapest-oil" tabindex="-1" class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0"><span role="text">Tips for finding the cheapest oil</span></h2></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Gormley said it&#x27;s important to buy oil in bulk, as the smaller order you place, the more you pay per litre.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">CCNI&#x27;s <a href="https://www.consumercouncil.org.uk/home-heating/price-checker" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">weekly oil price checker<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> allows you to see average prices for 300, 500 and 900 litres of oil, which gives consumers an idea of how much they should be spending before pricing local suppliers.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">For those who do not have a lump sum available to order oil, Mr Gormley suggested joining an <a href="https://www.nihe.gov.uk/housing-help/ni-energy-advice/oil-savings-network" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">oil buying club<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> where communities come together to buy oil in bulk and, hopefully, make a saving.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The NI Oil Federation also offers a <a href="http://nioil.com/paypoint/" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">pre-payment scheme<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>, while oil fuel stamps allow residents to budget and spread the cost by purchasing stamps from local retailers and using them to pay for their oil delivery.</p></div></div><div data-component="topic-list" class="ssrcss-1e4xw2r-TopicListWrapper etw6iwl1"><div class="ssrcss-113c0cq-StyledTagContainer ed0g1kj1"><div class="ssrcss-1pfbb52-TopicListHeaderWrapper etw6iwl0"><h2
